06/01/2024, 14:24 - Tanishq Mahajan: Basic Rules of Chess 
1) White Moves first
2) Always touch king first while castling
3) You can only castle when king hasn't moved or won't be under threat while castling
4) only 1 illegal move is allowed
5) play and press the clock with the same hand if not it is considered as illigal move
6) if you play in opponents time its a illegal move

Openings in Chess
For White
1) Italian Opening :- https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PL9RQPxG_e-LlwrRs1AbpHiQ4sAdERLfIf&si=mI0GfbPCyNGmVHw0
2) London Opening :- https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PL9RQPxG_e-Ln-2uIhSws3CO47PQlADUhx&si=FUzKwoDc6DixhToa

For Black
1)Carocan defence :- https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PL9RQPxG_e-LmXOjbqXE_Pccyy7pvRUI1O&si=YbwjsWK3EtARIHKY
2) French Defence :- https://youtube.com/playlist?list=PL9RQPxG_e-Lm9gKP5T7dzUuhw_D45SDLP&si=aTSf98S8WDqj3H6Y

Where to practice

1) Chess.com
2) lichess.org

For inter class competition, each department will be assigned with specific colour. IT: Yellow 
Mechanical: Red 
MCA: White
